 (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) (except for the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) The worship of Lord Surya has begun
 hindu dharm main kisi bhi parv kii shuruyaat snaan ke saath hi hoti he or yah parv bhi snaan yani nahaay-khaay ke saath shuru hua
 On the occasion of nahay-khay, the fasting women take the offerings made of pumpkin and rice after bathing and worshiping
 iske agle din kharnaa kii jaaegi or isi ke saath vrati mahilaon kaa 36 ghante kaa nirjala upwas shuru hoga jo guuruuvaar ko ugte surya ko arghya arpit karne ke baad samaapt hoga
 In the unique festival Chhath of the Atal Faith of the devotees, the first ray of the sun in the sixth and the last ray in the evening are offered to the Sun by offering it
 suryopasna kaa yah parv karthik maheene ke shukla paksh ke chaturthi se saptami tithi tak manaaya jaataa he
 It is called 'chhath' due to the fast of Surya Shashthi
 sukh-samruddhi or manovanchit fal dene vaale is parv ko purush or mahila samaan rup se manaate hai, parantu aam taur par vrath karne waalon main mahilaon kii sankhya adhik hoti he
 Till a few years ago, this festival was mainly celebrated in Bihar, Jharkhand and some areas of Uttar Pradesh, but now this festival is being celebrated all over the country
 chaar dinon kaa hota he chhath parvachath parv kaa prarambh karthik shukla paksh kii chaturth tithi se prarambh hota he tathaa saptami tithi ko is parv kaa samaapan hota he
 The festival starts with 'nahai-khay', on which day the Vratis take bath and eat Arva rice, gram dal and pumpkin vegetable
 is din khaane main sendha namak kaa prayog kiya jaataa he
 On the second day of nahay-khay, i
e
, fasting for the whole day of Kartik Shukla Paksha Panchami, taking a fast in the evening, bathing in the evening, preparing the prasad made of bread and jaggery made by ritual, worshiping Lord Bhaskar and receiving the offerings
 is puja ko 'kharnaa' kaha jaataa he
 On the next day, fasting on Kartik Shukla Paksha Shashthi Tithi (29th October this year), going to the river, pond, or other reservoirs in the evening, taking the prasadam, fruit, reed and other offerings in the Vrati basket (daura made of bamboo), in the evening, to the astral sun They offer it and offer arghya to the rising sun in the morning on the next day i
e
 on the seventh day, return to home and take food and water and 'paran' i
e
 break the fast
 chhath se judi prachlit lok kathaenek manyata ke anusaar bhagwaan ram or mata sita ne ravan vadh ke baad karthik shukla shashthee ko upwas kiya or suryadev kii aradhana kii or agle din yani saptami ko ugte surya kii puja kii or aashirwad praapt kiya
 According to another belief, Chhath started in the Mahabharata period and was first worshiped by Suryaputra Karna
 karn ang pradesh yani vartmaan bihar ke bhagalpur ke raja the
 Karna used to stand for hours in the water and offer Arghya to Suryadev and by his grace he became the ultimate warrior
 chhath main aaj bhi arghya dene kii parampara he
 In the Mahabharata period, there is mention of worshiping the Sun of the Pandavas by Bharatya Draupadi, who used to perform this puja regularly for the health and longevity of her family
 pracheen dharmik manyataon ke anusaar, is anupam mahaparv ko lekar kai kathaayen prachlit hai
 Chhath Devi is the sister of Sun God and Lord Sun is worshiped to please her

 paryaavaran mantralay ne company ke khilaaf yah aadesh somvaar ko jari kiya, jise mangalvaar ko saarvajanik kiya gaya he
 The Ministry stated that lcl's project violates the environmental impact assessment year 1994, 2004 and 2006 notifications
 pariyojna ke tahat hua nirmaan anaadhikrut he or paryaavaran ke prati nuksaandeh he
 The Ministry said that if LCL responds and if it provides relevant and reliable material to the Ministry to move forward in this matter, then the Ministry is ready to consider the company's project on merit basis

 There are usually three types of charges in the food bill

 Let us see all taxes and charges on food bills 1
 sarvice tex: food bill par sarvice tex kendra sarkaar vasuulati he
 This tax is levied on the services provided by the restaurant
 tex niyam ke mutabik yah tex restaurant dwaara food or bevarej ko chhodkar di ja rahi anya sevaaon par lagata he
 For example, this tax is levied on services like air conditioner, waiter, entertainment etc
 in restaurants
 maujuuda samay main deshbhar main 14 fisadi sarvice tex lagata he
 Also 0 on food bill
 5 fisadi krishi kalyaan tex or 0
 There is a 5 per cent Clean India tax
 yah tex sabhi restaurant ko sarkaar ke paas jamaa karana hota he or isliye restaurant is tex ko aapse vasuulakar aage badha detii hai
 2
 vailu aded tex: yah tex rajya sarkaron dwaara nirdhaarit hota he lihaaja isaki dar prayek rajya main alag-alag rahati he
 This tax is levied on the food and beverages served by the restaurant
 tex niyam ke mutabik yah tex sirf restaurant main taiyaar kiye gaye khaane or bevarej par lagaaya ja saktaa he
 Therefore, this tax does not cover cold drinks, liquor, billeries, etc
 served in restaurants as these products are made outside the restaurant

 This tax is levied by adding service charge to the food bill and does not include service tax
 3
 Service Charge: Now the third and most disputed charge is the service charge
 is charge kaa koi kanoonee praavdhaan nahin he
 However, this is included in the restaurant food bill as a global practice

 Usually the entire money collected from this charge is distributed among the waiters, managers and cleaning staff in the restaurant
 haalanki restaurant kaa yah saport staff masik selary par rahata he lekin restaurant is charge ko bataur park or bonus apane karmchaariyon main baant dete hai

 aapke food bill main is charge ke judane ke baad restaurant main aapako waiter ko tip dene kii jarurat nahin padati

 Due to having a dark circle: There can be many reasons behind being a dark circle
 kai baar bahut adhik tanaav lene kii vajah se ankhon ke neeche kaale ghere ban jate hai
 Apart from this, due to less sleep, changes in hormones, not having the right lifestyle or being genetic, dark circles also form under the eyes
 haalanki bazaar main kai aise beauty product maujuud hai jo ye daawa karte hai ki inke istemaal se dark sarkal dur ho jate hai lekin agar aapaki skin sensotive he to ye aapke liye khatarnaak bhi sabit ho sakate hai
 In such a situation, dark circles can be overcome by adopting these home remedies: 1
 dark sarkal dur karne ke liye tamaato ek acha upaay he
 This naturally works to eliminate dark circles under the eyes
 saath hi iske istemaal se skin fresh bani rahati he
 Mixing tomato juice with a few drops of lemon and applying it quickly helps
 2
 Potatoes can also be used to remove dark circles
 aalu ke ras ko bhi neembu kii kuch buundon ke saath mila len
 Applying this solution under the eyes with the help of cotton will remove the dark circles
 3
 Dark circles also disappear quickly with the use of cold T-bags
 tii-bag ko kuch der pani main dubokar rakh den
 After that keep it in the fridge to cool down
 kuch der baad ise nikaalkar ankhon par rakhkar let jaaen
 Doing this daily for 10 minutes will benefit
 4
 Blackness under the eyes is also removed by applying cold milk
 5
 Dry orange peel in sunlight and grind it
 is powder main thodi si maatra main gulab jal milakar lagane se kaale ghere khatm ho jaaenge
